p=0;for l=l,o do p=p+1;w[l]=n[p]end;for l=o+1,m[5][1]do w[l]=nil end end elseif(x<=5)then if(x==4)then local l=w[v[4]]if(l)then w[v[2]]=l;o=v[3]end elseif(x<=5)then w[v[2]][w[v[3]]]=w[v[4]]end
